Applications&quot;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;This comprehensive &lt;strong&gt;50-hour&lt;/strong&gt; course is designed to provide in-depth knowledge and hands-on understanding of three fundamental types of electrical machines: &lt;strong&gt;DC machines&lt;/strong&gt;, &lt;strong&gt;Synchronous machines&lt;/strong&gt;, and &lt;strong&gt;Induction machines&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Whether you are an electrical engineering student, a professional in the field, or someone seeking to enhance your expertise in electrical machines, &lt;strong&gt;this course will equip you with both theoretical foundations and practical applications crucial for mastering these machines.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course Structure:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;The course is divided into &lt;/em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;three comprehensive courses&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;, each focusing on a specific type of machine:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course # 1 :  DC Machines&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following topics are discussed in details:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Introduction to DC machine principles&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Construction and operating principles.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Armature reaction, commutation, and armature windings.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;DC generators types, features, and applications&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Performance characteristics and efficiency analysis of DC generators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;DC motors types, features, and applications&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Starting methods of DC motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Control methods, including speed control and torque regulation in DC motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;DC machine testing &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects and applications on DC machine in MATLAB.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course # 2 :  Synchronous Machines&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following topics are discussed in details:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Principles of synchronous machines&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous generators types, models, and characteristics&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Manufacturing of alternator windings&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Factors affecting the alternator voltage&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Role of governor control (ALFC) in alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Role of excitation control (AVR) in alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Types of exciters used in alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous generator testing&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Performance and characteristics of stand alone generator&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Behavior of alternator operating with large power system&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronization process of alternators with grid&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Parallel operation of alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;House diagram of alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous generator ratings&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Learn how to read the nameplate of alternator&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Capability diagram and P-Q chart of alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Complete analysis of salient pole alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Reluctance motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous motors principles, working, model, and analysis&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous condenser&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Starting of synchronous motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Complete design of synchronous machines&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Stator and rotor design with several design problems&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects on synchronous machines in MATLAB.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course # 3 :  Induction Machines&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Three phase induction motors overview&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Induction motors construction, types, model, and characteristics.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Starting methods of induction motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Direct online, Start-delta starter, auto-transformer starter, soft starter, Rotor resistance starter&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Speed control of induction motors (Speed drives)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;V- control,  F- control ,  V/F control, rotor resistance control, slip energy recovery control&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Variable frequency drives (VFD)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Complete study of single phase induction motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Realize different methods to start single phase induction motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Induction motors testing&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Induction generators (Types, applications, features)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects on induction machines in MATLAB.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course Materials and Resources:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;Detailed lecture notes and reference material .&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;900 lecture slides provided for you !!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Interactive quizzes and assignments for each course to reinforce learning.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;High quality video tutorials and demonstrations for simple understanding.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects on MATLAB to model machine performance in electric system&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;MATLAB Simulink files related to electrical machines provided for you !! in-depth knowledge and hands-on understanding of three fundamental types of electrical machines: &lt;strong&gt;DC machines&lt;/strong&gt;, &lt;strong&gt;Synchronous machines&lt;/strong&gt;, and &lt;strong&gt;Induction machines&lt;/strong&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Whether you are an electrical engineering student, a professional in the field, or someone seeking to enhance your expertise in /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course Structure:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;The course is divided into &lt;/em&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;three comprehensive courses&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;, each focusing on a specific type of machine:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br DC machine principles&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Construction and operating principles.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Armature reaction, commutation, and armature windings.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;DC generators types, features, and applications&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Performance characteristics and efficiency analysis of DC generators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;DC motors types, features, and applications&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Starting methods of DC motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Control methods, including speed control and torque regulation in DC motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;DC machine testing &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects and applications on DC machine in MATLAB.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course # 2 :  Synchronous Machines&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following topics windings&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Factors affecting the alternator voltage&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Role of governor control (ALFC) in alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Role of excitation control (AVR) in alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Types of exciters used in alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous generator testing&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Performance and characteristics of stand alone generator&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Behavior of alternator operating with large power system&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronization process of alternators with grid&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Parallel operation of diagram and P-Q chart of alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Complete analysis of salient pole alternators&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Reluctance motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous motors principles, working, model, and analysis&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Synchronous condenser&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Starting of synchronous motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Complete design of synchronous machines&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Stator and rotor design with several design problems&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects on synchronous machines in MATLAB.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Course # 3 :  Induction Machines&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Three phase induction motors overview&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Induction motors construction, types, model, and characteristics.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Starting methods of induction motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Direct online, Start-delta starter, auto-transformer starter, soft starter, Rotor resistance starter&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Speed control of induction motors (Speed drives)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;V- control,  F- control ,  V/F control, rotor resistance control, slip energy recovery control&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Variable frequency drives (VFD)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Complete study of single phase induction motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Realize different methods to start single phase induction motors&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Induction motors testing&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Induction generators (Types, applications, features)&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Practical projects on induction machines in class="ud-text-sm component-margin" data-purpose="course-description"><h2 data-purpose="description-title" class="ud-heading-xl course-description-module-scss-module___l52bq__description-header">Description</h2><div class="_container_kolij_42" data-expanded="false"><div class="_content_kolij_32 _with-gradient_kolij_57" style="max-height:13.8125rem"><div tabindex="-1"><div data-purpose="safely-set-inner-html:description:description" data-testid="safely-set-inner-html:description:description"><p><em>Hi and welcome everyone to our course</em> <strong><em>" Mastering Electrical Machines: Theory, Design, Applications"</em></strong></p><p><br /></p><p>This comprehensive <strong>50-hour</strong> course is designed to provide in-depth knowledge and hands-on understanding of three fundamental types of electrical machines: <strong>DC machines</strong>, <strong>Synchronous machines</strong>, and <strong>Induction machines</strong>.</p><p>Whether you are an electrical engineering student, a professional in the field, or someone seeking to enhance your expertise in electrical machines, <strong>this course will equip you with both theoretical foundations and practical applications crucial for mastering these machines.</strong></p><p><br /></p><ul><li><p><strong><em>Course Structure:</em></strong></p></li></ul><p><em>The course is divided into </em><strong><em>three comprehensive courses</em></strong><em>, each focusing on a specific type of machine:</em></p><p><br /></p><p><strong><em>Course # 1 :  DC Machines</em></strong></p><p>The following topics are discussed in details:</p><p>Introduction to DC machine principles</p><p>Construction and operating principles.</p><p>Armature reaction, commutation, and armature windings.</p><p>DC generators types, features, and applications</p><p>Performance characteristics and efficiency analysis of DC generators</p><p>DC motors types, features, and applications</p><p>Starting methods of DC motors</p><p>Control methods, including speed control and torque regulation in DC motors</p><p>DC machine testing </p><p>Practical projects and applications on DC machine in MATLAB.</p><p><br /></p><p><strong><em>Course # 2 :  Synchronous Machines</em></strong></p><p>The following topics are discussed in details:</p><p>Principles of synchronous machines</p><p>Synchronous generators types, models, and characteristics</p><p>Manufacturing of alternator windings</p><p>Factors affecting the alternator voltage</p><p>Role of governor control (ALFC) in alternators</p><p>Role of excitation control (AVR) in alternators</p><p>Types of exciters used in alternators</p><p>Synchronous generator testing</p><p>Performance and characteristics of stand alone generator</p><p>Behavior of alternator operating with large power system</p><p>Synchronization process of alternators with grid</p><p>Parallel operation of alternators</p><p>House diagram of alternators</p><p>Synchronous generator ratings</p><p>Learn how to read the nameplate of alternator</p><p>Capability diagram and P-Q chart of alternators</p><p>Complete analysis of salient pole alternators</p><p>Reluctance motors</p><p>Synchronous motors principles, working, model, and analysis</p><p>Synchronous condenser</p><p>Starting of synchronous motors</p><p>Complete design of synchronous machines</p><p>Stator and rotor design with several design problems</p><p>Practical projects on synchronous machines in MATLAB.</p><p><br /></p><p><strong><em>Course # 3 :  Induction Machines</em></strong></p><p>Three phase induction motors overview</p><p>Induction motors construction, types, model, and characteristics.</p><p>Starting methods of induction motors</p><p>Direct online, Start-delta starter, auto-transformer starter, soft starter, Rotor resistance starter</p><p>Speed control of induction motors (Speed drives)</p><p>V- control,  F- control ,  V/F control, rotor resistance control, slip energy recovery control</p><p>Variable frequency drives (VFD)</p><p>Complete study of single phase induction motors</p><p>Realize different methods to start single phase induction motors</p><p>Induction motors testing</p><p>Induction generators (Types, applications, features)</p><p>Practical projects on induction machines in MATLAB.</p><p><br /></p><ul><li><p><strong><em>Course Materials and Resources:</em></strong></p></li></ul><p>Detailed lecture notes and reference material .</p><p>900 lecture slides provided for you !!</p><p>Interactive quizzes and assignments for each course to reinforce learning.</p><p>High quality video tutorials and demonstrations for simple understanding.</p><p>Practical projects on MATLAB to model machine performance in electric system</p><p>MATLAB Simulink files related to electrical machines provided for you !! </p><p>ـــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــــ</p><p><strong><em>By the end of this course, you will be able to cover all the principles of operation, design, and performance analysis of these machines through realizing real-world examples, industrial applications, and troubleshooting techniques.</em></strong></p><p><br /></p><p>Thank you very much for you time.</p><p>See you in the course !</p><p><br /></p></div><div class="course-description-module-scss-module___l52bq__audience" data-purpose="target-audience"><h2 class="ud-heading-xl course-description-module-scss-module___l52bq__audience-title">Who this course
